DST Registers and variables

A description of all DST registers and variables in the projectdatabase.

Complete DST variable list

To get the complete DST variable list, click this link.

This will take you to an Excel file on GitHub.com with the complete variable list. To download the file, click the download button in the top right corner of the page.

Registers from Statistics Denmark

Below you will find a full describtion of all DST registers and variables in the project database
